CLI Plugin Activation Fix (`src/cli/manage.js`, lines 66-68)\n\nAdded validation after auto-complete:\n\n```javascript\nplugin = await plugins.autocomplete(plugin);\n\n// NEW: Validate plugin ID after auto-complete\nif (!pluginNamePattern.test(plugin)) {\n    throw new Error('[[error:invalid-plugin-id]]');\n}\n```\n\n**Impact:** CLI users now get immediate feedback when attempting to activate plugins with malformed names. Invalid identifiers like `'not-a-plugin'` or `'\\t\\nnodebb-plugin'` are properly rejected.\n\n### 2. Socket.IO Admin Plugin Ordering Fix (`src/socket.io/admin/plugins.js`, lines 45-49)\n\nAdded validation for each plugin in the order array:\n\n```javascript\ndata = data.filter(plugin => plugin && plugin.name);\n// NEW: Validate each plugin ID\nfor (const plugin of data) {\n    if (!pluginNamePattern.test(plugin.name)) {\n        throw new Error('[[error:invalid-plugin-id]]');\n    }\n}\nawait Promise.all(data.map(plugin => db.sortedSetAdd('plugins:active', plugin.order || 0, plugin.name)));\n```\n\n**Impact:** Admin panel users cannot inadvertently add malformed plugin names when reordering plugins. The system validates each entry before database operations.\n\n### 3. Theme Activation Fix (`src/meta/themes.js`, lines 88-91)\n\nAdded validation of theme IDs against the plugin naming pattern:\n\n```javascript\nThemes.set = async (data) => {\n    switch (data.type) {\n        case 'local': {\n            // NEW: Validate theme ID against plugin naming pattern\n            if (!pluginNamePattern.test(data.id)) {\n                throw new Error('[[error:invalid-plugin-id]]');\n            }\n            // ... rest of the function\n```\n\n**Impact:** Themes cannot be activated with invalid identifiers. Since themes are stored in the `plugins:active` sorted set, they must follow the same naming conventions.\n\n## Validation Examples\n\n### Valid Plugin IDs (All Pass)\n- `nodebb-plugin-markdown`\n- `nodebb-plugin-dbsearch`\n- `nodebb-theme-persona`\n- `@myorg/nodebb-plugin-custom`\n- `@scope/nodebb-theme-dark`\n\n### Invalid Plugin IDs (All Rejected)\n- `notaplugin` - Missing required prefix\n- `not-a-plugin` - Missing `nodebb-` prefix\n- `'\\t\\nnodebb-plugin'` - Contains whitespace\n- `'  nodebb-plugin-test'` - Leading whitespace\n- `'nodebb-plugin-test  '` - Trailing whitespace\n- `'nodebb-invalid-type-test'` - Invalid type (not theme, plugin, widget, or rewards)\n- `''` - Empty string\n- `'plugin-with-whitespace in name'` - Contains spaces in the middle\n\n## Testing\n\nAll fixes maintain backward compatibility with existing tests:\n- Existing tests for `plugins.toggleActive()` continue to pass (already had validation)\n- New validation prevents previously-unvalidated paths from accepting malformed identifiers\n- Error messages use the standard NodeBB error key `[[error:invalid-plugin-id]]` for consistency\n\n## Error Handling\n\nAll three fixes throw the same error message that the existing `toggleActive()` function uses:\n```javascript\nthrow new Error('[[error:invalid-plugin-id]]');\n```\n\nThis provides consistent user feedback across all plugin activation methods.\n\n## Security Considerations\n\n1. **Input Validation**: All plugin identifiers are now validated against the strict naming pattern before database operations\n2. **Early Rejection**: Invalid identifiers are rejected at the application layer before reaching the database\n3. **Consistency**: All activation paths now enforce the same validation rules\n4. **No Breaking Changes**: The validation only rejects identifiers that should never have been accepted in the first place\n\n## Files Modified\n\n1. `src/cli/manage.js` - Added validation after auto-complete\n2. `src/socket.io/admin/plugins.js` - Added validation in orderActivePlugins\n3. `src/meta/themes.js` - Added validation in Themes.set\n\nAll changes are minimal, focused, and maintain the existing code style and error handling patterns.\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":9,"cache_creation_input_tokens":354,"cache_read_input_tokens":95248,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":354},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"8b7b85da-a8f1-460a-aaca-9da86734652a","uuid":"4a243da7-f399-4079-9a8a-fe8083507192"}

Invalid identifiers like `'not-a-plugin'` or `'\\t\\nnodebb-plugin'` are properly rejected.\n\n### 2. Socket.IO Admin Plugin Ordering Fix (`src/socket.io/admin/plugins.js`, lines 45-49)\n\nAdded validation for each plugin in the order array:\n\n```javascript\ndata = data.filter(plugin => plugin && plugin.name);\n// NEW: Validate each plugin ID\nfor (const plugin of data) {\n    if (!pluginNamePattern.test(plugin.name)) {\n        throw new Error('[[error:invalid-plugin-id]]');\n    }\n}\nawait Promise.all(data.map(plugin => db.sortedSetAdd('plugins:active', plugin.order || 0, plugin.name)));\n```\n\n**Impact:** Admin panel users cannot inadvertently add malformed plugin names when reordering plugins. The system validates each entry before database operations.\n\n### 3. Theme Activation Fix (`src/meta/themes.js`, lines 88-91)\n\nAdded validation of theme IDs against the plugin naming pattern:\n\n```javascript\nThemes.set = async (data) => {\n    switch (data.type) {\n        case 'local': {\n            // NEW: Validate theme ID against plugin naming pattern\n            if (!pluginNamePattern.test(data.id)) {\n                throw new Error('[[error:invalid-plugin-id]]');\n            }\n            // ... rest of the function\n```\n\n**Impact:** Themes cannot be activated with invalid identifiers. Since themes are stored in the `plugins:active` sorted set, they must follow the same naming conventions.\n\n## Validation Examples\n\n### Valid Plugin IDs (All Pass)\n- `nodebb-plugin-markdown`\n- `nodebb-plugin-dbsearch`\n- `nodebb-theme-persona`\n- `@myorg/nodebb-plugin-custom`\n- `@scope/nodebb-theme-dark`\n\n### Invalid Plugin IDs (All Rejected)\n- `notaplugin` - Missing required prefix\n- `not-a-plugin` - Missing `nodebb-` prefix\n- `'\\t\\nnodebb-plugin'` - Contains whitespace\n- `'  nodebb-plugin-test'` - Leading whitespace\n- `'nodebb-plugin-test  '` - Trailing whitespace\n- `'nodebb-invalid-type-test'` - Invalid type (not theme, plugin, widget, or rewards)\n- `''` - Empty string\n- `'plugin-with-whitespace in name'` - Contains spaces in the middle\n\n## Testing\n\nAll fixes maintain backward compatibility with existing tests:\n- Existing tests for `plugins.toggleActive()` continue to pass (already had validation)\n- New validation prevents previously-unvalidated paths from accepting malformed identifiers\n- Error messages use the standard NodeBB error key `[[error:invalid-plugin-id]]` for consistency\n\n## Error Handling\n\nAll three fixes throw the same error message that the existing `toggleActive()` function uses:\n```javascript\nthrow new Error('[[error:invalid-plugin-id]]');\n```\n\nThis provides consistent user feedback across all plugin activation methods.\n\n## Security Considerations\n\n1. **Input Validation**: All plugin identifiers are now validated against the strict naming pattern before database operations\n2. **Early Rejection**: Invalid identifiers are rejected at the application layer before reaching the database\n3. **Consistency**: All activation paths now enforce the same validation rules\n4. **No Breaking Changes**: The validation only rejects identifiers that should never have been accepted in the first place\n\n## Files Modified\n\n1. `src/cli/manage.js` - Added validation after auto-complete\n2. `src/socket.io/admin/plugins.js` - Added validation in orderActivePlugins\n3. `src/meta/themes.js` - Added validation in Themes.set\n\nAll changes are minimal, focused, and maintain the existing code style and error handling patterns.\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
